## Уровень 17: Нейроархитектура сознания

### 17.1 Топологические свойства сознательных сетей

#### Algebraic topology нейронных пространств

**Фундаментальные работы:**
- Curto, C. (2017). "What can topology tell us about the neural code?" *Bulletin of the American Mathematical Society*, 54(1), 63-78.
- Ghrist, R. (2008). "Barcodes: the persistent topology of data." *Bulletin of the American Mathematical Society*, 45(1), 61-75.
- Dabaghian, Y., Mémoli, F., Frank, L., & Carlsson, G. (2012). "A topological paradigm for hippocampal spatial map formation using persistent homology." *PLoS Computational Biology*, 8(8), e1002581.

**Специализированные исследования:**
- Petri, G., Expert, P., Turkheimer, F., Carhart-Harris, R., Nutt, D., Hellyer, P. J., & Vaccarino, F. (2014). "Homological scaffolds of brain functional networks." *Journal of The Royal Society Interface*, 11(101), 20140873.
- Sizemore, A. E., Giusti, C., Kahn, A., Vettel, J. M., Betzel, R. F., & Bassett, D. S. (2018). "Cliques and cavities in the human connectome." *Journal of Computational Neuroscience*, 44(1), 115-145.
- Reimann, M. W., Nolte, M., Scolamiero, M., Turner, K., Perin, R., Chindemi, G., ... & Markram, H. (2017). "Cliques of neurons bound into cavities provide a missing link between structure and function." *Frontiers in Computational Neuroscience*, 11, 48.

#### Homological scaffolds в brain networks

**Основополагающие статьи:**
- Lord, L. D., Expert, P., Fernandes, H. M., Petri, G., Van Hartevelt, T. J., Vaccarino, F., ... & Turkheimer, F. E. (2016). "Insights into brain architectures from the homological scaffolds of functional connectivity networks." *Frontiers in Systems Neuroscience*, 10, 85.
- Saggar, M., Sporns, O., Gonzalez-Castillo, J., Bandettini, P. A., Carlsson, G., Glover, G., & Reiss, A. L. (2018). "Towards a new approach to reveal dynamical organization of the brain using topological data analysis." *Nature Communications*, 9(1), 1399.
- Stolz, B. J., Harrington, H. A., & Porter, M. A. (2017). "Persistent homology of time-dependent functional networks constructed from coupled time series." *Chaos*, 27(4), 047410.

#### Persistent homology conscious states

**Методологические основы:**
- Carlsson, G. (2009). "Topology and data." *Bulletin of the American Mathematical Society*, 46(2), 255-308.
- Perea, J. A. (2019). "Topological time series analysis." *Notices of the American Mathematical Society*, 66(5), 686-694.
- Chazal, F., & Michel, B. (2021). "An introduction to topological data analysis: fundamental and practical aspects for data scientists." *Frontiers in Artificial Intelligence*, 4, 667963.

**Применения к сознанию:**
- Varley, T. F., Sporns, O., Puce, A., & Beggs, J. (2020). "Differential effects of propofol and ketamine on critical brain dynamics." *PLoS Computational Biology*, 16(12), e1008418.
- Reardon, P. K., Seidlitz, J., Vandekar, S., Liu, S., Raznahan, A., Vértes, P. E., ... & Alexander-Bloch, A. F. (2018). "Normative brain size variation and brain shape diversity in humans." *Nature Communications*, 9(1), 1-19.

#### Topological data analysis сознания

**Теоретические основы:**
- Wasserman, L. (2018). "Topological data analysis." *Annual Review of Statistics and Its Application*, 5, 501-532.
- Otter, N., Porter, M. A., Tillmann, U., Grindrod, P., & Harrington, H. A. (2017). "A roadmap for the computation of persistent homology." *EPJ Data Science*, 6(1), 17.
- Chazal, F., & Michel, B. (2021). "An introduction to topological data analysis: fundamental and practical aspects for data scientists." *Frontiers in Artificial Intelligence*, 4, 667963.

**Нейробиологические приложения:**
- Geniesse, C., Sporns, O., Petri, G., & Saggar, M. (2019). "Generating dynamical neuroimaging spatiotemporal representations (DyNiSR) using topological data analysis." *Network Neuroscience*, 3(3), 763-778.
- Phinyomark, A., Ibanez-Marcelo, E., & Petri, G. (2017). "Resting-state fMRI functional connectivity: big data preprocessing pipelines and topological data analysis." *IEEE Transactions on Big Data*, 3(4), 415-428.

#### Geometric deep learning для brain connectivity

**Методологические инновации:**
- Bronstein, M. M., Bruna, J., LeCun, Y., Szlam, A., & Vandergheynst, P. (2017). "Geometric deep learning: going beyond Euclidean data." *IEEE Signal Processing Magazine*, 34(4), 18-42.
- Kipf, T. N., & Welling, M. (2016). "Semi-supervised classification with graph convolutional networks." *arXiv preprint arXiv:1609.02907*.
- Defferrard, M., Bresson, X., & Vandergheynst, P. (2016). "Convolutional neural networks on graphs with fast localized spectral filtering." *Advances in Neural Information Processing Systems*, 29.

**Применения к нейроданным:**
- Parisot, S., Ktena, S. I., Ferrante, E., Lee, M., Guerrero, R., Glocker, B., & Rueckert, D. (2018). "Disease prediction using graph convolutional networks: application to autism spectrum disorder and Alzheimer's disease." *Medical Image Analysis*, 48, 117-130.
- Ktena, S. I., Parisot, S., Ferrante, E., Rajchl, M., Lee, M., Glocker, B., & Rueckert, D. (2018). "Metric learning with spectral graph convolutions on brain connectivity networks." *NeuroImage*, 169, 431-442.

### 17.2 Фрактальная организация сознания

#### Self-similar structures в нейронных сетях

**Фундаментальные исследования:**
- Bassett, D. S., & Bullmore, E. (2006). "Small-world brain networks." *The Neuroscientist*, 12(6), 512-523.
- Bullmore, E., & Sporns, O. (2009). "Complex brain networks: graph theoretical analysis of structural and functional systems." *Nature Reviews Neuroscience*, 10(3), 186-198.
- Sporns, O. (2013). "Network attributes for segregation and integration in the human brain." *Current Opinion in Neurobiology*, 23(2), 162-171.

**Фрактальные свойства мозга:**
- Mandelbrot, B. B. (1982). "The fractal geometry of nature." *W.H. Freeman and Company*.
- Caserta, F., Stanley, H. E., Eldred, W. D., Daccord, G., Hausman, R. E., & Nittmann, J. (1990). "Physical mechanisms underlying neurite outgrowth: a quantitative analysis of neuronal shape." *Physical Review Letters*, 64(1), 95.
- Jelinek, H. F., & Fernandez, E. (1998). "Neurons and fractals: how reliable and useful are calculations of fractal dimensions?" *Journal of Neuroscience Methods*, 81(1-2), 9-18.

#### Scale-free networks и сознание

**Теоретические основы:**
- Barabási, A. L., & Albert, R. (1999). "Emergence of scaling in random networks." *Science*, 286(5439), 509-512.
- Albert, R., & Barabási, A. L. (2002). "Statistical mechanics of complex networks." *Reviews of Modern Physics*, 74(1), 47.
- Newman, M. E. (2005). "Power laws, Pareto distributions and Zipf's law." *Contemporary Physics*, 46(5), 323-351.

**Нейробиологические применения:**
- Eguiluz, V. M., Chialvo, D. R., Cecchi, G. A., Baliki, M., & Apkarian, A. V. (2005). "Scale-free brain functional networks." *Physical Review Letters*, 94(1), 018102.
- Achard, S., Salvador, R., Whitcher, B., Suckling, J., & Bullmore, E. (2006). "A resilient, low-frequency, small-world human brain functional network with highly connected association cortical hubs." *Journal of Neuroscience*, 26(1), 63-72.
- van den Heuvel, M. P., & Sporns, O. (2013). "Network hubs in the human brain." *Trends in Cognitive Sciences*, 17(12), 683-696.

#### Fractal dimension нейронной активности

**Методологические подходы:**
- Higuchi, T. (1988). "Approach to an irregular time series on the basis of the fractal theory." *Physica D*, 31(2), 277-283.
- Katz, M. J. (1988). "Fractals and the analysis of waveforms." *Computers in Biology and Medicine*, 18(3), 145-156.
- Sevcik, C. (1998). "A procedure to estimate the fractal dimension of waveforms." *arXiv preprint physics/9802054*.

**Нейрофизиологические исследования:**
- Lutzenberger, W., Preissl, H., & Pulvermüller, F. (1995). "Fractal dimension of electroencephalographic time series and underlying brain processes." *Biological Cybernetics*, 73(5), 477-482.
- Stam, C. J. (2005). "Nonlinear dynamical analysis of EEG and MEG: review of an emerging field." *Clinical Neurophysiology*, 116(10), 2266-2301.
- Kesić, S., & Spasić, S. Z. (2016). "Application of Higuchi's fractal dimension from basic to clinical neurophysiology: a review." *Computer Methods and Programs in Biomedicine*, 133, 55-70.

#### Multiscale organization conscious processes

**Теоретические рамки:**
- Deco, G., Jirsa, V. K., & McIntosh, A. R. (2011). "Emerging concepts for the dynamical organization of resting-state activity in the brain." *Nature Reviews Neuroscience*, 12(1), 43-56.
- Breakspear, M. (2017). "Dynamic models of large-scale brain activity." *Nature Neuroscience*, 20(3), 340-352.
- Honey, C. J., Sporns, O., Cammoun, L., Gigandet, X., Thiran, J. P., Meuli, R., & Hagmann, P. (2009). "Predicting human resting-state functional connectivity from structural connectivity." *Proceedings of the National Academy of Sciences*, 106(6), 2035-2040.

**Мультимасштабная динамика:**
- Palva, J. M., & Palva, S. (2012). "Infra-slow fluctuations in electrophysiological recordings, blood-oxygenation-level-dependent signals, and psychophysical time series." *NeuroImage*, 62(4), 2201-2211.
- Betzel, R. F., & Bassett, D. S. (2017). "Multi-scale brain networks." *NeuroImage*, 160, 73-83.
- Zorick, T., & Mandelkern, M. A. (2013). "Multifractal detrended fluctuation analysis of human EEG: preliminary investigation and comparison with the wavelet transform modulus maxima technique." *PLoS One*, 8(7), e68360.

#### Hierarchical modularity в мозге

**Модульная организация:**
- Newman, M. E. (2006). "Modularity and community structure in networks." *Proceedings of the National Academy of Sciences*, 103(23), 8577-8582.
- Fortunato, S. (2010). "Community detection in graphs." *Physics Reports*, 486(3-5), 75-174.
- Sporns, O., & Betzel, R. F. (2016). "Modular brain networks." *Annual Review of Psychology*, 67, 613-640.

**Иерархическая структура:**
- Meunier, D., Lambiotte, R., & Bullmore, E. T. (2010). "Modular and hierarchically modular organization of brain networks." *Frontiers in Neuroscience*, 4, 200.
- Bassett, D. S., Porter, M. A., Wymbs, N. F., Grafton, S. T., Carlson, J. M., & Mucha, P. J. (2011). "Dynamic reconfiguration of human brain networks during learning." *Proceedings of the National Academy of Sciences*, 108(18), 7641-7646.
- Park, H. J., & Friston, K. (2013). "Structural and functional brain networks: from connections to cognition." *Science*, 342(6158), 1238411.

#### Nature exposure и restoration effects

**Теория восстановления внимания:**
- Kaplan, S. (1995). "The restorative benefits of nature: toward an integrative framework." *Journal of Environmental Psychology*, 15(3), 169-182.
- Ulrich, R. S. (1984). "View through a window may influence recovery from surgery." *Science*, 224(4647), 420-421.
- Berman, M. G., Jonides, J., & Kaplan, S. (2008). "The cognitive benefits of interacting with nature." *Psychological Science*, 19(12), 1207-1212.

**Нейробиологические механизмы:**
- Bratman, G. N., Hamilton, J. P., Hahn, K. S., Daily, G. C., & Gross, J. J. (2015). "Nature experience reduces rumination and subgenual prefrontal cortex activation." *Proceedings of the National Academy of Sciences*, 112(28), 8567-8572.
- Aspinall, P., Mavros, P., Coyne, R., & Roe, J. (2015). "The urban brain: analysing outdoor physical activity with mobile EEG." *British Journal of Sports Medicine*, 49(4), 272-276.
- Dadvand, P., Nieuwenhuijsen, M. J., Esnaola, M., Forns, J., Basagaña, X., Alvarez-Pedrerol, M., ... & Sunyer, J. (2015). "Green spaces and cognitive development in primary schoolchildren." *Proceedings of the National Academy of Sciences*, 112(26), 7937-7942.

#### Noise pollution и cognitive performance

**Шумовое загрязнение:**
- Basner, M., Babisch, W., Davis, A., Brink, M., Clark, C., Janssen, S., & Stansfeld, S. (2014). "Auditory and non-auditory effects of noise on health." *The Lancet*, 383(9925), 1325-1332.
- Stansfeld, S. A., & Matheson, M. P. (2003). "Noise pollution: non-auditory effects on health." *British Medical Bulletin*, 68(1), 243-257.
- Clark, C., & Stansfeld, S. A. (2007). "The effect of transportation noise on health and cognitive development: a review of recent evidence." *International Journal of Comparative Psychology*, 20(2).

**Когнитивные эффекты:**
- Hygge, S., Evans, G. W., & Bullinger, M. (2002). "A prospective study of some effects of aircraft noise on cognitive performance in schoolchildren." *Psychological Science*, 13(5), 469-474.
- Shield, B. M., & Dockrell, J. E. (2008). "The effects of environmental and classroom noise on the academic attainments of primary school children." *The Journal of the Acoustical Society of America*, 123(1), 133-144.

#### Social density effects на нейронные сети

**Социальная скученность:**
- Epstein, Y. M. (1981). "Crowding stress and human behavior." *Journal of Social Issues*, 37(1), 126-144.
- Evans, G. W., & McCoy, J. M. (1998). "When buildings don't work: the role of architecture in human health." *Journal of Environmental Psychology*, 18(1), 85-94.
- Regoeczi, W. C. (2003). "When context matters: a multilevel analysis of household and neighbourhood crowding on aggression and withdrawal." *Journal of Environmental Psychology*, 23(4), 457-470.

**Нейронные корреляты:**
- Sandi, C., & Haller, J. (2015). "Stress and the social brain: behavioural effects and neurobiological mechanisms." *Nature Reviews Neuroscience*, 16(5), 290-304.
- Tost, H., Champagne, F. A., & Meyer-Lindenberg, A. (2015). "Environmental influence in the brain, human welfare and mental health." *Nature Neuroscience*, 18(10), 1421-1431.

#### Green spaces и mental health

**Зеленые пространства и благополучие:**
- Hartig, T., Mitchell, R., De Vries, S., & Frumkin, H. (2014). "Nature and health." *Annual Review of Public Health*, 35, 207-228.
- Gascon, M., Triguero-Mas, M., Martínez, D., Dadvand, P., Forns, J., Plasència, A., & Nieuwenhuijsen, M. J. (2015). "Mental health benefits of long-term exposure to residential green and blue spaces: a systematic review." *International Journal of Environmental Research and Public Health*, 12(4), 4354-4379.
- Kondo, M. C., Fluehr, J. M., McKeon, T., & Branas, C. C. (2018). "Urban green space and its impact on human health." *International Journal of Environmental Research and Public Health*, 15(3), 445.

**Механизмы действия:**
- Van den Berg, M., Wendel-Vos, W., Van Poppel, M., Kemper, H., Van Mechelen, W., & Maas, J. (2015). "Health benefits of green spaces in the living environment: a systematic review of epidemiological studies." *Urban Forestry & Urban Greening*, 14(4), 806-816.
- Twohig-Bennett, C., & Jones, A. (2018). "The health benefits of the great outdoors: a systematic review and meta-analysis of greenspace exposure and health outcomes." *Environmental Research*, 166, 628-637.
- Rojas-Rueda, D., Nieuwenhuijsen, M. J., Gascon, M., Perez-Leon, D., & Mudu, P. (2019). "Green spaces and mortality: a systematic review and meta-analysis of cohort studies." *The Lancet Planetary Health*, 3(11), e469-e477.

## Уровень 19: Нейробиология творчества

### 19.1 Творческие процессы и сознание

#### Default mode network в творческом мышлении

**Основополагающие работы:**
- Beaty, R. E., Benedek, M., Silvia, P. J., & Schacter, D. L. (2016). Creative cognition and brain network dynamics. *Trends in Cognitive Sciences*, 20(2), 87-95.
- Buckner, R. L., Andrews‐Hanna, J. R., & Schacter, D. L. (2008). The brain's default network: anatomy, function, and relevance to disease. *Annals of the New York Academy of Sciences*, 1124(1), 1-38.
- Christoff, K., Irving, Z. C., Fox, K. C., Spreng, R. N., & Andrews-Hanna, J. R. (2016). Mind-wandering as spontaneous thought: a dynamic framework. *Nature Reviews Neuroscience*, 17(11), 718-731.

**Специализированные исследования:**
- Ellamil, M., Dobson, C., Beeman, M., & Christoff, K. (2012). Evaluative and generative modes of thought during the creative process. *NeuroImage*, 59(2), 1783-1794.
- Limb, C. J., & Braun, A. R. (2008). Neural substrates of spontaneous musical performance: an fMRI study of jazz improvisation. *PLoS One*, 3(2), e1679.
- Liu, S., Erkkinen, M. G., Healey, M. L., Xu, Y., Swett, K. E., Chow, H. M., & Braun, A. R. (2015). Brain activity and connectivity during poetry composition: toward a multidimensional model of the creative process. *Human Brain Mapping*, 36(9), 3351-3372.

#### Divergent thinking и нейронная flexibility

**Классические работы:**
- Guilford, J. P. (1967). *The nature of human intelligence*. McGraw-Hill.
- Torrance, E. P. (1966). *Torrance tests of creative thinking*. Personnel Press.

**Нейровизуализационные исследования:**
- Benedek, M., Jauk, E., Sommer, M., Arendasy, M., & Neubauer, A. C. (2014). Intelligence, creativity, and cognitive control: The common and differential involvement of executive functions in intelligence and creativity. *Intelligence*, 46, 73-83.
- Fink, A., Grabner, R. H., Benedek, M., Reishofer, G., Hauswirth, V., Fally, M., ... & Neubauer, A. C. (2009). The creative brain: Investigation of brain activity during creative problem solving by means of EEG and fMRI. *Human Brain Mapping*, 30(3), 734-748.
- Jung, R. E., Mead, B. S., Carrasco, J., & Flores, R. A. (2013). The structure of creative cognition in the human brain. *Frontiers in Human Neuroscience*, 7, 330.

**Сетевые исследования:**
- Beaty, R. E., Benedek, M., Kaufman, S. B., & Silvia, P. J. (2015). Default and executive network coupling supports creative idea production. *Scientific Reports*, 5(1), 1-14.
- Kenett, Y. N., Anaki, D., & Faust, M. (2014). Investigating the structure of semantic networks in low and high creative persons. *Frontiers in Human Neuroscience*, 8, 407.

#### Insight moments и sudden awareness

**Фундаментальные работы:**
- Kounios, J., & Beeman, M. (2014). The cognitive neuroscience of insight. *Annual Review of Psychology*, 65, 71-93.
- Jung-Beeman, M., Bowden, E. M., Haberman, J., Frymiare, J. L., Arambel-Liu, S., Greenblatt, R., ... & Kounios, J. (2004). Neural activity when people solve verbal problems with insight. *PLoS Biology*, 2(4), e97.

**Электрофизиологические исследования:**
- Sandkühler, S., & Bhattacharya, J. (2008). Deconstructing insight: EEG correlates of insightful problem solving. *PLoS One*, 3(1), e1459.
- Shen, W., Yuan, Y., Liu, C., & Luo, J. (2016). In search of the 'Aha!' experience: Elucidating the emotionality of insight problem-solving. *British Journal of Psychology*, 107(2), 281-298.

**Нейрохимические аспекты:**
- Subramaniam, K., Kounios, J., Parrish, T. B., & Jung-Beeman, M. (2009). A brain mechanism for facilitation of insight by positive affect. *Journal of Cognitive Neuroscience*, 21(3), 415-432.

#### Artistic creativity и brain networks

**Музыкальное творчество:**
- Bengtsson, S. L., Csíkszentmihályi, M., & Ullén, F. (2007). Cortical regions involved in piano playing. *Cerebral Cortex*, 17(4), 886-893.
- Pinho, A. L., De Manzano, Ö., Fransson, P., Eriksson, H., & Ullén, F. (2014). Connecting to create: expertise in musical improvisation is associated with increased functional connectivity between premotor and prefrontal areas. *Journal of Neuroscience*, 34(18), 6156-6163.

**Визуальное искусство:**
- Solso, R. L. (2001). Brain activities in a skilled versus a novice artist: an fMRI study. *Leonardo*, 34(1), 31-34.
- Vartanian, O., & Goel, V. (2004). Neuroanatomical correlates of aesthetic preference for paintings. *Neuroreport*, 15(5), 893-897.

**Литературное творчество:**
- Shah, C., Erhard, K., Ortheil, H. J., Kaza, E., Kessler, C., & Lotze, M. (2013). Neural correlates of creative writing: an fMRI study. *Human Brain Mapping*, 34(5), 1088-1101.

#### Flow states и optimal performance

**Основополагающие работы:**
- Csikszentmihalyi, M. (1990). *Flow: The psychology of optimal experience*. Harper & Row.
- Csikszentmihalyi, M. (1996). *Creativity: Flow and the psychology of discovery and invention*. HarperCollins.

**Нейробиологические исследования:**

- Ulrich, M., Keller, J., Hoenig, K., Waller, C., & Grön, G. (2014). Neural correlates of experimentally induced flow experiences. *NeuroImage*, 86, 194-202.

### 19.2 Нейронные механизмы инноваций

#### Conceptual blending в creative cognition

**Теоретические основы:**
- Fauconnier, G., & Turner, M. (2002). *The way we think: Conceptual blending and the mind's hidden complexities*. Basic Books.

**Нейрокогнитивные исследования:**

**Нейровизуализационные исследования:**

#### Serendipity и unexpected connections

**Теоретические работы:**
- Copeland, S. (2019). On serendipity in science: discovery at the intersection of chance and wisdom. *Synthese*, 196(6), 2385-2406.
- Pina e Cunha, M., Clegg, S. R., & Mendonça, S. (2010). On serendipity and organizing. *European Management Journal*, 28(5), 319-330.

**Нейрокогнитивные исследования:**
- Kounios, J., & Beeman, M. (2009). The Aha! moment: the cognitive neuroscience of insight. *Current Directions in Psychological Science*, 18(4), 210-216.
- Ritter, S. M., & Dijksterhuis, A. (2014). Creativity—the unconscious foundations of the incubation period. *Frontiers in Human Neuroscience*, 8, 215.

#### Cognitive flexibility и creative problem-solving

**Фундаментальные работы:**
- Diamond, A. (2013). Executive functions. *Annual Review of Psychology*, 64, 135-168.
- Miyake, A., Friedman, N. P., Emerson, M. J., Witzki, A. H., Howerter, A., & Wager, T. D. (2000). The unity and diversity of executive functions and their contributions to complex "frontal lobe" tasks. *Cognitive Psychology*, 41(1), 49-100.

**Связь с творчеством:**
- Zabelina, D. L., & Robinson, M. D. (2010). Child's play: Facilitating the originality of creative output by a priming manipulation. *Psychology of Aesthetics, Creativity, and the Arts*, 4(1), 57-65.
- Zmigrod, S., Colzato, L. S., & Hommel, B. (2015). Stimulating creativity: modulation of convergent and divergent thinking by transcranial direct current stimulation (tDCS). *Creativity Research Journal*, 27(4), 353-360.

#### Expertise effects на creative processes

**Экспертиза и творчество:**
- Ericsson, K. A., Krampe, R. T., & Tesch-Römer, C. (1993). The role of deliberate practice in the acquisition of expert performance. *Psychological Review*, 100(3), 363-406.
- Weisberg, R. W. (2006). *Creativity: Understanding innovation in problem solving, science, invention, and the arts*. John Wiley & Sons.

**Нейробиологические исследования:**
- Ellamil, M., Dobson, C., Beeman, M., & Christoff, K. (2012). Evaluative and generative modes of thought during the creative process. *NeuroImage*, 59(2), 1783-1794.
- Ritter, S. M., Kühn, S., Müller, B. C., van Baaren, R. B., Brass, M., & Dijksterhuis, A. P. (2014). The creative brain: corepresenting schema violations enhances TPJ activity and boosts cognitive flexibility. *Creativity Research Journal*, 26(2), 144-150.

## Уровень 20: Нейроэпигенетика сознания

- Halder, R., Hennion, M., Vidal, R. O., Shomroni, O., Rahman, R. U., Rajput, A., ... & Fischer, A. (2016). DNA methylation changes in plasticity genes accompany the formation and maintenance of memory. *Nature Neuroscience*, 19(1), 102-110.

#### Histone modifications и gene expression

**Нейроспецифические исследования:**

**Связь с обучением и памятью:**

Spatial memory consolidation is associated with induction of several lysine-acetyltransferase (histone acetyltransferase) expression in rat hippocampus. *Neuropsychopharmacology*, 35(13), 2521-2537.
- Peixoto, L., & Abel, T. (2013). The role of histone acetylation in memory formation and cognitive impairments. *Neuropsychopharmacology*, 38(1), 62-76.

#### Non-coding RNAs в нейронной пластичности

**MicroRNAs:**
- Schratt, G. M., Tuebing, F., Nigh, E. A., Kane, C. G., Sabatini, M. E., Kiebler, M., & Greenberg, M. E. (2006). A brain-specific microRNA regulates dendritic spine development. *Nature*, 439(7074), 283-289.
- Vo, N., Klein, M. E., Varlamova, O., Keller, D. M., Yamamoto, T., Goodman, R. H., & Impey, S. (2005). A cAMP-response element binding protein-induced microRNA regulates neuronal morphogenesis. *Proceedings of the National Academy of Sciences*, 102(45), 16426-16431.

**Long non-coding RNAs:**
- Bernard, D., Prasanth, K. V., Tripathi, V., Colasse, S., Nakamura, T., Xuan, Z., ... & Spector, D. L. (2010). A long nuclear-retained non-coding RNA regulates synaptogenesis by modulating gene expression. *EMBO Journal*, 29(18), 3082-3093.
- Qureshi, I. A., Mattick, J. S., & Mehler, M. F. (2010). Long non-coding RNAs in nervous system function and disease. *Brain Research*, 1338, 20-35.

- You, X., Vlatkovic, I., Babic, A., Will, T., Epstein, I., Tushev, G., ... & Rajewsky, N. (2015). Neural circular RNAs are derived from synaptic genes and regulated by development and plasticity. *Nature Neuroscience*, 18(4), 603-610.

#### Chromatin remodeling и memory formation

#### Epigenetic clocks в нейронном старении

**Обратимость маркеров:**

## Дополнительные междисциплинарные источники

### Методологические работы:
- Lövdén, M., Wenger, E., Mårtensson, J., Lindenberger, U., & Bäckman, L. (2013). Structural brain plasticity in adult learning and development. *Neuroscience & Biobehavioral Reviews*, 37(9), 2296-2310.
- Zatorre, R. J., Fields, R. D., & Johansen-Berg, H. (2012). Plasticity in gray and white: neuroimaging changes in brain structure during learning. *Nature Neuroscience*, 15(4), 528-536.

### Обзорные работы:
- Berdasco, M., & Esteller, M. (2019). Clinical epigenetics: seizing opportunities for translation. *Nature Reviews Genetics*, 20(2), 109-127.
- Gräff, J., & Tsai, L. H. (2013). Histone acetylation: molecular mnemonics on the chromatin. *Nature Reviews Neuroscience*, 14(2), 97-111.

### Технические ресурсы:
- ENCODE Project Consortium. (2012). An integrated encyclopedia of DNA elements in the human genome. *Nature*, 489(7414), 57-74.
- Roadmap Epigenomics Consortium. (2015). Integrative analysis of 111 reference human epigenomes. *Nature*, 518(7539), 317-330.

## Уровень 21: Нейрореабилитация сознания

### 21.1 Восстановление сознательных функций

#### Neuroplasticity-based rehabilitation

**Ключевые источники:**
- **Merzenich, M. M.** (2013). *Soft-wired: How the new science of brain plasticity can change your life*. Parnassus Publishing.
- **Kleim, J. A., & Jones, T. A.** (2008). Principles of experience-dependent neural plasticity: implications for rehabilitation after brain damage. *Journal of Speech, Language, and Hearing Research*, 51(1), S225-S239.
- **Cramer, S. C., Sur, M., Dobkin, B. H., et al.** (2011). Harnessing neuroplasticity for clinical applications. *Brain*, 134(6), 1591-1609.
- **Ganguly, K., & Poo, M. M.** (2013). Activity-dependent neural plasticity from bench to bedside. *Neuron*, 80(3), 729-741.
- **Dayan, E., & Cohen, L. G.** (2011). Neuroplasticity subserving motor skill learning. *Neuron*, 72(3), 443-454.

#### Constraint-induced movement therapy

**Ключевые источники:**
- **Taub, E., Uswatte, G., & Pidikiti, R.** (1999). Constraint-induced movement therapy: a new family of techniques with broad application to physical rehabilitation. *Journal of Rehabilitation Research and Development*, 36(3), 237-251.
- **Wolf, S. L., Winstein, C. J., Miller, J. P., et al.** (2006). Effect of constraint-induced movement therapy on upper extremity function 3 to 9 months after stroke. *JAMA*, 296(17), 2095-2104.
- **Morris, D. M., Taub, E., & Mark, V. W.** (2006). Constraint-induced movement therapy: characterizing the intervention protocol. *Europa Medicophysica*, 42(3), 257-268.
- **Kunkel, A., Kopp, B., Müller, G., et al.** (1999). Constraint-induced movement therapy for motor recovery in chronic stroke patients. *Archives of Physical Medicine and Rehabilitation*, 80(6), 624-628.

#### Cognitive rehabilitation protocols

**Ключевые источники:**
- **Cicerone, K. D., Langenbahn, D. M., Braden, C., et al.** (2011). Evidence-based cognitive rehabilitation: updated review of the literature from 2003 through 2008. *Archives of Physical Medicine and Rehabilitation*, 92(4), 519-530.
- **Wilson, B. A.** (2008). Neuropsychological rehabilitation. *Annual Review of Clinical Psychology*, 4, 141-162.
- **Sohlberg, M. M., & Mateer, C. A.** (2001). *Cognitive rehabilitation: An integrative neuropsychological approach*. Guilford Press.
- **Robertson, I. H., & Murre, J. M.** (1999). Rehabilitation of brain damage: brain plasticity and principles of guided recovery. *Psychological Bulletin*, 125(5), 544-575.

#### Virtual reality в реабилитации

**Ключевые источники:**
- **Laver, K. E., Lange, B., George, S., et al.** (2017). Virtual reality for stroke rehabilitation. *Cochrane Database of Systematic Reviews*, 11, CD008349.
- **Rizzo, A., & Kim, G. J.** (2005). A SWOT analysis of the field of virtual reality rehabilitation and therapy. *Presence: Teleoperators & Virtual Environments*, 14(2), 119-146.
- **Weiss, P. L., Katz, N., & Kizony, R.** (2006). Virtual reality in neurorehabilitation. *Textbook of Neural Repair and Rehabilitation*, 182-197.
- **Holden, M. K.** (2005). Virtual environments for motor rehabilitation: review. *CyberPsychology & Behavior*, 8(3), 187-211.
- **Adamovich, S. V., Fluet, G. G., Tunik, E., & Merians, A. S.** (2009). Sensorimotor training in virtual reality: a review. *NeuroRehabilitation*, 25(1), 29-44.

#### Neurofeedback и biofeedback approaches

**Ключевые источники:**
- **Dempster, T.** (2012). The use of EEG biofeedback/neurofeedback in psychiatric and developmental disorders. *Psychiatric Times*, 29(6), 20-22.
- **Gruzelier, J. H.** (2014). EEG-neurofeedback for optimising performance. I: A review of cognitive and affective outcome in healthy participants. *Neuroscience & Biobehavioral Reviews*, 44, 124-141.
- **Strehl, U.** (2014). What learning theories can teach us in designing neurofeedback treatments. *Frontiers in Human Neuroscience*, 8, 894.
- **Sitaram, R., Ros, T., Stoeckel, L., et al.** (2017). Closed-loop brain training: the science of neurofeedback. *Nature Reviews Neuroscience*, 18(2), 86-100.

### 21.2 Нейропротезирование сознания

#### Cochlear implants и auditory consciousness

**Ключевые источники:**
- **Wilson, B. S., & Dorman, M. F.** (2008). Cochlear implants: a remarkable past and a brilliant future. *Hearing Research*, 242(1-2), 3-21.
- **Zeng, F. G., Rebscher, S., Harrison, W., et al.** (2008). Cochlear implants: system design, integration, and evaluation. *IEEE Reviews in Biomedical Engineering*, 1, 115-142.
- **Loizou, P. C.** (1998). Mimicking the human ear. *IEEE Signal Processing Magazine*, 15(5), 101-130.
- **Rubinstein, J. T.** (2004). How cochlear implants encode speech. *Current Opinion in Otolaryngology & Head and Neck Surgery*, 12(5), 444-448.
- **Drennan, W. R., & Rubinstein, J. T.** (2008). Music perception in cochlear implant users and its relationship with psychophysical capabilities. *Journal of Rehabilitation Research and Development*, 45(5), 779-789.

#### Retinal prosthetics и visual awareness

**Ключевые источники:**
- **Humayun, M. S., Dorn, J. D., da Cruz, L., et al.** (2012). Interim results from the international trial of Second Sight's visual prosthesis. *Ophthalmology*, 119(4), 779-788.
- **Weiland, J. D., Cho, A. K., & Humayun, M. S.** (2011). Retinal prostheses: current clinical results and future needs. *Ophthalmology*, 118(11), 2227-2237.
- **Stingl, K., Bartz-Schmidt, K. U., Besch, D., et al.** (2013). Artificial vision with wirelessly powered subretinal electronic implant alpha-IMS. *Proceedings of the Royal Society B*, 280(1757), 20130077.
- **Dagnelie, G.** (2013). Retinal implants: emergence of a multidisciplinary field. *Current Opinion in Neurology*, 26(1), 75-83.

#### Motor neuroprosthetics и sense of agency

**Ключевые источники:**
- **Wolpaw, J. R., Birbaumer, N., McFarland, D. J., et al.** (2002). Brain-computer interfaces for communication and control. *Clinical Neurophysiology*, 113(6), 767-791.
- **Hochberg, L. R., Bacher, D., Jarosiewicz, B., et al.** (2012). Reach and grasp by people with tetraplegia using a neurally controlled robotic arm. *Nature*, 485(7398), 372-375.
- **Collinger, J. L., Wodlinger, B., Downey, J. E., et al.** (2013). High-performance neuroprosthetic control by an individual with tetraplegia. *The Lancet*, 381(9866), 557-564.
- **Bensmaia, S. J., & Miller, L. E.** (2014). Restoring sensorimotor function through intracortical interfaces: progress and looming challenges. *Nature Reviews Neuroscience*, 15(5), 313-325.

#### Cognitive prosthetics и memory enhancement

**Ключевые источники:**
- **Berger, T. W., Hampson, R. E., Song, D., et al.** (2011). A cortical neural prosthesis for restoring and enhancing memory. *Journal of Neural Engineering*, 8(4), 046017.
- **Hampson, R. E., Song, D., Chan, R. H., et al.** (2012). Closing the loop for memory prosthesis: detecting the role of hippocampal neural ensembles using nonlinear dynamics. *IEEE Transactions on Neural Systems and Rehabilitation Engineering*, 20(4), 510-525.
- **Deadwyler, S. A., Berger, T. W., Sweatt, A. J., et al.** (2013). Donor/recipient enhancement of memory in rat hippocampus. *Frontiers in Systems Neuroscience*, 7, 120.
- **Laxton, A. W., Tang-Wai, D. F., McAndrews, M. P., et al.** (2010). A phase I trial of deep brain stimulation of memory circuits in Alzheimer's disease. *Annals of Neurology*, 68(4), 521-534.

#### Sensory substitution devices

**Ключевые источники:**
- **Bach-y-Rita, P., & Kercel, S. W.** (2003). Sensory substitution and the human-machine interface. *Trends in Cognitive Sciences*, 7(12), 541-546.
- **Lenay, C., Gapenne, O., Hanneton, S., et al.** (2003). Sensory substitution: limits and perspectives. *Touching for Knowing*, 275-292.
- **Nagel, S. K., Carl, C., Kringe, T., et al.** (2005). Beyond sensory substitution—learning the sixth sense. *Journal of Neural Engineering*, 2(4), R13.
- **Proulx, M. J., Stoerig, P., Ludowig, E., & Knoll, I.** (2008). Seeing 'where' through the ears: effects of learning-by-doing and long-term sensory deprivation on localization based on image-to-sound substitution. *PLoS One*, 3(3), e1840.

## Уровень 22: Нейроэстетика сознания

### 22.1 Эстетический опыт и сознание

#### Beauty perception и reward systems

**Ключевые источники:**
- **Kawabata, H., & Zeki, S.** (2004). Neural correlates of beauty. *Journal of Neurophysiology*, 91(4), 1699-1705.
- **Aharon, I., Etcoff, N., Ariely, D., et al.** (2001). Beautiful faces have variable reward value: fMRI and behavioral evidence. *Neuron*, 32(3), 537-551.
- **Vartanian, O., & Goel, V.** (2004). Neuroanatomical correlates of aesthetic preference for paintings. *Neuroreport*, 15(5), 893-897.
- **Ishizu, T., & Zeki, S.** (2011). Toward a brain-based theory of beauty. *PLoS One*, 6(7), e21852.
- **Brown, S., Gao, X., Tisdelle, L., et al.** (2011). Naturalizing aesthetics: brain areas for aesthetic appraisal across sensory modalities. *NeuroImage*, 58(1), 250-258.

#### Aesthetic emotions и neural correlates

**Ключевые источники:**
- **Vessel, E. A., Starr, G. G., & Rubin, N.** (2012). The brain on art: intense aesthetic experience activates the default mode network. *Frontiers in Human Neuroscience*, 6, 66.
- **Nadal, M., Munar, E., Marty, G., & Cela-Conde, C. J.** (2010). Visual complexity and beauty appreciation: explaining the divergence of results. *Empirical Studies of the Arts*, 28(2), 173-191.
- **Leder, H., Belke, B., Oeberst, A., & Augustin, D.** (2004). A model of aesthetic appreciation and aesthetic judgments. *British Journal of Psychology*, 95(4), 489-508.
- **Cupchik, G. C., Vartanian, O., Crawley, A., & Mikulis, D. J.** (2009). Viewing artworks: contributions of cognitive control and perceptual facilitation to aesthetic experience. *Brain and Cognition*, 70(1), 84-91.

#### Art appreciation и default mode network

**Ключевые источники:**
- **Vessel, E. A., Starr, G. G., & Rubin, N.** (2013). Art reaches within: aesthetic experience, the self and the default mode network. *Frontiers in Neuroscience*, 7, 258.
- **Cela-Conde, C. J., Marty, G., Maestú, F., et al.** (2004). Activation of the prefrontal cortex in the human visual aesthetic perception. *Proceedings of the National Academy of Sciences*, 101(16), 6321-6325.
- **Di Dio, C., Macaluso, E., & Rizzolatti, G.** (2007). The golden beauty: brain response to classical and renaissance sculptures. *PLoS One*, 2(11), e1201.
- **Jacobsen, T., Schubotz, R. I., Höfel, L., & Cramon, D. Y. V.** (2006). Brain correlates of aesthetic judgment of beauty. *NeuroImage*, 29(1), 276-285.

#### Musical consciousness и temporal processing

**Ключевые источники:**
- **Koelsch, S.** (2012). *Brain and music*. John Wiley & Sons.
- **Peretz, I., & Zatorre, R. J.** (2005). Brain organization for music processing. *Annual Review of Psychology*, 56, 89-114.
- **Zatorre, R. J., Chen, J. L., & Penhune, V. B.** (2007). When the brain plays music: auditory-motor interactions in music perception and production. *Nature Reviews Neuroscience*, 8(7), 547-558.
- **Levitin, D. J., & Tirovolas, A. K.** (2009). Current advances in the cognitive neuroscience of music. *Annals of the New York Academy of Sciences*, 1156(1), 211-231.
- **Salimpoor, V. N., Benovoy, M., Larcher, K., et al.** (2011). Anatomically distinct dopamine release during anticipation and experience of peak emotion to music. *Nature Neuroscience*, 14(2), 257-262.

#### Synesthetic experiences в искусстве

**Ключевые источники:**
- **Ramachandran, V. S., & Hubbard, E. M.** (2001). Synaesthesia–a window into perception, thought and language. *Journal of Consciousness Studies*, 8(12), 3-34.
- **Rouw, R., & Scholte, H. S.** (2007). Increased structural connectivity in grapheme-color synesthesia. *Nature Neuroscience*, 10(6), 792-797.
- **Simner, J., & Carmichael, D. A.** (2015). Is synaesthesia a dominantly female trait? *Cognitive Neuroscience*, 6(2-3), 68-76.
- **Brang, D., & Ramachandran, V. S.** (2011). Survival of the synesthesia gene: why do people hear colors and taste words? *PLoS Biology*, 9(11), e1001205.

### 22.2 Культурные различия в эстетике

#### Cross-cultural aesthetic preferences

**Ключевые источники:**
- **Chatterjee, A.** (2014). *The aesthetic brain: How we evolved to desire beauty and enjoy art*. Oxford University Press.
- **Vessel, E. A., Maurer, N., Denker, A. H., & Starr, G. G.** (2018). Stronger shared taste for natural aesthetic domains than for artifacts of human culture. *Cognition*, 179, 121-131.
- **Masuda, T., Gonzalez, R., Kwan, L., & Nisbett, R. E.** (2008). Culture and aesthetic preference: comparing the attention to context of East Asians and Americans. *Personality and Social Psychology Bulletin*, 34(9), 1260-1275.
- **Höfel, L., & Jacobsen, T.** (2007). Electrophysiological indices of processing aesthetics: spontaneous or intentional processes? *International Journal of Psychophysiology*, 65(1), 20-31.

#### Cultural neuroscience эстетического опыта

**Ключевые источники:**
- **Kitayama, S., & Uskul, A. K.** (2011). Culture, mind, and the brain: current evidence and future directions. *Annual Review of Psychology*, 62, 419-449.
- **Han, S., & Northoff, G.** (2008). Culture-sensitive neural substrates of human cognition: a transcultural neuroimaging approach. *Nature Reviews Neuroscience*, 9(8), 646-654.
- **Chiao, J. Y.** (2009). Cultural neuroscience: a once and future discipline. *Progress in Brain Research*, 178, 287-304.
- **Freeman, J. B., Rule, N. O., Adams Jr, R. B., & Ambady, N.** (2009). Culture shapes a mesolimbic response to signals of dominance and subordination that associates with behavior. *NeuroImage*, 47(1), 353-359.

#### Evolutionary aesthetics и brain evolution

**Ключевые источники:**
- **Dutton, D.** (2009). *The art instinct: Beauty, pleasure, and human evolution*. Oxford University Press.
- **Miller, G. F.** (2001). *The mating mind: How sexual choice shaped the evolution of human nature*. Anchor Books.
- **Pinker, S.** (1997). *How the mind works*. W. W. Norton & Company.
- **Dissanayake, E.** (2008). The arts after Darwin: does art have an origin and adaptive function? *World Art Studies: Exploring Concepts and Approaches*, 241-263.

#### Neuroaesthetics различных art forms

**Ключевые источники:**
- **Zeki, S.** (1999). *Inner vision: An exploration of art and the brain*. Oxford University Press.
- **Ramachandran, V. S., & Hirstein, W.** (1999). The science of art: a neurological theory of aesthetic experience. *Journal of Consciousness Studies*, 6(6-7), 15-51.
- **Livingstone, M.** (2002). *Vision and art: the biology of seeing*. Harry N. Abrams.
- **Kandel, E. R.** (2012). *The age of insight: the quest to understand the unconscious in art, mind, and brain*. Random House.

#### Aesthetic development across lifespan

**Ключевые источники:**
- **Winner, E.** (1982). *Invented worlds: The psychology of the arts*. Harvard University Press.
- **Parsons, M. J.** (1987). *How we understand art: A cognitive developmental account of aesthetic experience*. Cambridge University Press.
- **Gardner, H.** (1990). *Art education and human development*. Getty Publications.
- **Davis, J. H.** (2008). Why our schools need the arts. Teachers College Press.

## Дополнительные высокоцитируемые источники

### Специализированные журналы:
- **Frontiers in Human Neuroscience** - нейрореабилитация
- **Journal of NeuroEngineering and Rehabilitation** - нейропротезирование
- **Psychology of Aesthetics, Creativity, and the Arts** - нейроэстетика
- **Empirical Studies of the Arts** - эмпирические исследования искусства
- **Neurorehabilitation and Neural Repair** - нейрореабилитация

### Обзорные статьи высокого уровня:
- **Cramer, S. C.** (2008). Repairing the human brain after stroke: I. Mechanisms of spontaneous recovery. *Annals of Neurology*, 63(3), 272-287.
- **Chatterjee, A., & Vartanian, O.** (2014). Neuroaesthetics. *Trends in Cognitive Sciences*, 18(7), 370-375.
- **Lebedev, M. A., & Nicolelis, M. A.** (2017). Brain-machine interfaces: from basic science to neuroprosthetics and neurorehabilitation. *Physiological Reviews*, 97(2), 767-837.

### Междисциплинарные источники:
- **Reardon, S.** (2016). 'Brain doping' may improve athletes' performance. *Nature*, 531(7594), 283-284.
- **Ienca, M., & Andorno, R.** (2017). Towards new human rights in the age of neuroscience and neurotechnology. *Life Sciences, Society and Policy*, 13(1), 5.
- **Yudell, M., Roberts, D., DeSalle, R., & Tishkoff, S.** (2016). Taking race out of human genetics. *Science*, 351(6273), 564-565.
